\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
A TOML array. 

\textbackslash{}detail The interface of this type is modeled after std\+::vector, with some additional considerations made for the heterogeneous nature of a TOML array.

\textbackslash{}godbolt\{sj\+K4da\}

\textbackslash{}cpp

toml\+::table tbl = toml\+::parse(R"{}(     arr = \mbox{[}1, 2, 3, 4, \textquotesingle{}five\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} )"{}sv);

// get the element as an array toml\+::array\& arr = \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}tbl.\doxylink{classarray_ae355770b27d72e41a7dca38378ff0c94}{get\+\_\+as$<$toml\+::array$>$}("{}arr"{}); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

// increment each element with visit() for (auto\&\& elem \+: arr) \{ elem.\+visit(\mbox{[}\mbox{]}(auto\&\& el) noexcept \{ if constexpr (toml\+::is\+\_\+number$<$decltype(el)$>$) (\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}el)++; else if constexpr (toml\+::is\+\_\+string$<$decltype(el)$>$) el = "{}six"{}sv; \}); \} std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

// add and remove elements arr.\+push\+\_\+back(7); arr.\+push\+\_\+back(8.\+0f); arr.\+push\+\_\+back("{}nine"{}sv); arr.\+erase(arr.\+cbegin()); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

// emplace elements arr.\+emplace\+\_\+back("{}ten"{}); arr.\+emplace\+\_\+back$<$toml\+::array$>$(11, 12.\+0); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out \mbox{[} 1, 2, 3, 4, \textquotesingle{}five\textquotesingle{} \mbox{]} \mbox{[} 2, 3, 4, 5, \textquotesingle{}six\textquotesingle{} \mbox{]} \mbox{[} 3, 4, 5, \textquotesingle{}six\textquotesingle{}, 7, 8.\+0, \textquotesingle{}nine\textquotesingle{} \mbox{]} \mbox{[} 3, 4, 5, \textquotesingle{}six\textquotesingle{}, 7, 8.\+0, \textquotesingle{}nine\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}ten\textquotesingle{}, \mbox{[} 11, 12.\+0 \mbox{]} \mbox{]} \textbackslash{}eout

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{erase()}{erase()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_adf515bb7a6b8ce6b14bf86c8961a63cb}{TOML\+\_\+\+EXPORTED\+\_\+\+MEMBER\+\_\+\+FUNCTION}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classarray_adc01054d5dfc4deee603ecaf9dfab71a}{iterator}} array\+::erase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classarray_ade84b39cb55e9f1496ec98f2aac6a983}{const\+\_\+iterator}}}]{first,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classarray_ade84b39cb55e9f1496ec98f2aac6a983}{const\+\_\+iterator}}}]{last }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Removes the elements in the range \mbox{[}first, last) from the array. 

\textbackslash{}detail \textbackslash{}cpp auto arr = toml\+::array\{ 1, "{}bad"{}, "{}karma"{} 2 \}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

arr.\+erase(arr.\+cbegin() + 1, arr.\+cbegin() + 3); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out \mbox{[} 1, \textquotesingle{}bad\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}karma\textquotesingle{}, 3 \mbox{]} \mbox{[} 1, 3 \mbox{]} \textbackslash{}eout


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em first} & Iterator to the first element being erased. \\
\hline
{\em last} & Iterator to the one-\/past-\/the-\/last element being erased.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Iterator to the first element immediately following the last removed element. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{flatten()}{flatten()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_adf515bb7a6b8ce6b14bf86c8961a63cb}{TOML\+\_\+\+EXPORTED\+\_\+\+MEMBER\+\_\+\+FUNCTION}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classarray}{array}} \& array\+::flatten (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) \&}



Flattens this array, recursively hoisting the contents of child arrays up into itself. 

\textbackslash{}detail \textbackslash{}cpp

auto arr = toml\+::array\{ 1, 2, toml\+::array\{ 3, 4, toml\+::array\{ 5 \} \}, 6, toml\+::array\{\} \}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

arr.\+flatten(); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out \mbox{[} 1, 2, \mbox{[} 3, 4, \mbox{[} 5 \mbox{]} \mbox{]}, 6, \mbox{[}\mbox{]} \mbox{]} \mbox{[} 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6 \mbox{]} \textbackslash{}eout

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Arrays inside child tables are not flattened.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A reference to the array. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Func $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classarray}{array}} \& array\+::for\+\_\+each (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Func \&\&}]{visitor }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) \&\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Invokes a visitor on each element in the array. 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Func} & A callable type invocable with one of the following signatures\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{_classes_2lib_2raylib_2src_2external_2glad_8h_a18ae3ab36a07e388833b568cfdfa90c8}{func(elem, index)}} 
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{_classes_2lib_2raylib_2src_2external_2glad_8h_a18ae3ab36a07e388833b568cfdfa90c8}{func(elem)}} 
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{_classes_2lib_2raylib_2src_2external_2glad_8h_a18ae3ab36a07e388833b568cfdfa90c8}{func(index, elem)}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}Where\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily elem} will recieve the element as it\textquotesingle{}s concrete type with cvref-\/qualifications matching the array 
\item {\ttfamily index} will recieve a {\ttfamily size\+\_\+t} indicating the element\textquotesingle{}s index 
\end{DoxyItemize}Visitors returning {\ttfamily bool} (or something convertible to {\ttfamily bool}) will cause iteration to stop if they return {\ttfamily false}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em visitor} & The visitor object.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A reference to the array.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\textbackslash{}cpp toml\+::array arr\{ 0, 1, 2, 3.\+0, "{}four"{}, "{}five"{}, 6 \};

// select only the integers using a strongly-\/typed visitor arr.\+for\+\_\+each(\mbox{[}\mbox{]}(toml\+::value$<$int64\+\_\+t$>$\& elem) \{ std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} elem \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}, "{}; \}); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

// select all the numeric values using a generic visitor + is\+\_\+number$<$$>$ metafunction arr.\+for\+\_\+each(\mbox{[}\mbox{]}(auto\&\& elem) \{ if constexpr (toml\+::is\+\_\+number$<$decltype(elem)$>$) std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} elem \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}, "{}; \}); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

// select all the numeric values until we encounter something non-\/numeric arr.\+for\+\_\+each(\mbox{[}\mbox{]}(auto\&\& elem) \{ if constexpr (toml\+::is\+\_\+number$<$decltype(elem)$>$) \{ std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} elem \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}, "{}; return true; // "{}keep going"{} \} else return false; // "{}stop!"{}

\}); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

\textbackslash{}ecpp \textbackslash{}out 0, 1, 2, 6, 0, 1, 2, 3.\+0, 6, 0, 1, 2, 3.\+0, \textbackslash{}eout

Inserts a new element at a specific position in the array. 

\textbackslash{}detail \textbackslash{}cpp auto arr = toml\+::array\{ 1, 3 \}; arr.\+insert(arr.\+cbegin() + 1, "{}two"{}); arr.\+insert(arr.\+cend(), toml\+::array\{ 4, 5 \}); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out \mbox{[} 1, \textquotesingle{}two\textquotesingle{}, 3, \mbox{[} 4, 5 \mbox{]} \mbox{]} \textbackslash{}eout

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
The return value will always be {\ttfamily \doxylink{classarray_a2027254bbe0a3e797c461a0b2446f656}{end()}} if the input value was a null toml\+::node\+\_\+view, because no insertion can take place. This is the only circumstance in which this can occur. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Elem\+Type $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classarray_adc01054d5dfc4deee603ecaf9dfab71a}{iterator}} array\+::replace (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classarray_ade84b39cb55e9f1496ec98f2aac6a983}{const\+\_\+iterator}}}]{pos,  }\item[{Elem\+Type \&\&}]{val,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_a0c7177c8470bcc9d80d5b97c482f4a86}{value\+\_\+flags}}}]{flags = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_ab28140ef75c3f18305fb795d6a7917c5}{preserve\+\_\+source\+\_\+value\+\_\+flags}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Replaces the element at a specific position in the array with a different value. 

\textbackslash{}detail \textbackslash{}cpp auto arr = toml\+::array\{ 1, 2, 3 \}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; arr.\+replace(arr.\+cbegin() + 1, "{}two"{}); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out \mbox{[} 1, 2, 3 \mbox{]} \mbox{[} 1, \textquotesingle{}two\textquotesingle{}, 3 \mbox{]} \textbackslash{}eout


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Elem\+Type} & toml\+::node, toml\+::node\+\_\+view, toml\+::table, toml\+::array, or a native TOML value type (or a type promotable to one). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pos} & The insertion position. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The node or value being inserted. \\
\hline
{\em flags} & Value flags to apply to new values.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\textbackslash{}conditional\+\_\+return\{Valid input\} An iterator to the replaced element. \textbackslash{}conditional\+\_\+return\{Input is a null toml\+::node\+\_\+view\} \doxylink{classarray_a2027254bbe0a3e797c461a0b2446f656}{end()}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
The return value will always be {\ttfamily \doxylink{classarray_a2027254bbe0a3e797c461a0b2446f656}{end()}} if the input value was a null toml\+::node\+\_\+view, because no replacement can take place. This is the only circumstance in which this can occur. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily array\+::\+TOML\+\_\+\+CONSTRAINED\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{(sizeof...(Elem\+Types) $>$ 0\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}!std\+::is\+\_\+same\+\_\+v$<$ impl\+::remove\+\_\+cvref$<$ Elem\+Type $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{classarray}{array}} $>$)}]{,  }\item[{typename Elem\+Type}]{,  }\item[{typename...}]{Elem\+Types }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) \&\&}



Constructs an array with one or more initial elements. 

\textbackslash{}detail \textbackslash{}cpp auto arr = toml\+::array\{ 1, 2.\+0, "{}three"{}sv, toml\+::array\{ 4, 5 \} \}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out \mbox{[} 1, 2.\+0, \textquotesingle{}three\textquotesingle{}, \mbox{[} 4, 5 \mbox{]} \mbox{]} \textbackslash{}eout

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
If you need to construct an array with one child array element, the array\textquotesingle{}s move constructor will take precedence and perform a move-\/construction instead. You can use toml\+::inserter to suppress this behaviour\+: \textbackslash{}cpp // desired result\+: \mbox{[} \mbox{[} 42 \mbox{]} \mbox{]} auto bad = toml\+::array\{ toml\+::array\{ 42 \} \} auto good = toml\+::array\{ toml\+::inserter\{ toml\+::array\{ 42 \} \} \} std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}bad\+: "{} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} bad \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}good\+:"{} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} good \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out bad\+: \mbox{[} 42 \mbox{]} good\+: \mbox{[} \mbox{[} 42 \mbox{]} \mbox{]} \textbackslash{}eout


\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{truncate()}{truncate()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_adf515bb7a6b8ce6b14bf86c8961a63cb}{TOML\+\_\+\+EXPORTED\+\_\+\+MEMBER\+\_\+\+FUNCTION}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_classes_2lib_2raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_e_g_l_2eglext_8h_a0f7193911e632cd84da4082d5c628fe3}{void}} array\+::truncate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_classes_2lib_2include_2stddef_8h_aa9d55e2f20e580b7445617d0d12fff6e}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{new\+\_\+size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Shrinks the array to the given size. 

\textbackslash{}detail \textbackslash{}godbolt\{rx\+Ez\+K5\}

\textbackslash{}cpp auto arr = toml\+::array\{ 1, 2, 3 \}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

arr.\+truncate(5); // no-\/op std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

arr.\+truncate(1); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} arr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out \mbox{[} 1, 2, 3 \mbox{]} \mbox{[} 1, 2, 3 \mbox{]} \mbox{[} 1\mbox{]} \textbackslash{}eout

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Does nothing if the requested size is larger than or equal to the current size. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
